The subject of privacy has attracted the attention of scholars from a wide variety of disciplines, including philosophy, 
sociology, political science, and law. To avoid swamping the reader with an impossibly vast list of sources, I have restricted 
this inventory to reasonableโand accessibleโproportions, omitting references to the prodigious quantity of periodical literature 
that grapples with this kaleidoscopic concept (the most essential of which are cited in the โReferencesโ section).
